                                    1502=            =    Ÿ  The size of a page buffer is controlled by the constant below.  Ÿ
                                    1503=            =    Ÿ  If you change this, it's probably safest to re-assemble all of  Ÿ
                                    1504=            =    Ÿ  WYLBUR.  Any value between 8K and 32K-1 is acceptable.          Ÿ
                                    1505=            =    Ÿ                                                                  Ÿ
                                    1506=            =    Ÿ  23476 is a good size for a 3380 device (2 records per track).   Ÿ
                                    1507=            =    Ÿ  15476 is a good size for a 3380 device (3 records per track).   Ÿ
                                    1508=            =    Ÿ  27998 is a good size for a 3390 device.                         Ÿ
                                    1509=            =    Ÿ  18452 is a good size for a 3390 device.                         Ÿ
                                    1510=            =    Ÿ                                                                  Ÿ
                                    1511=            =    Ÿ  In order to optimize on memory usage the page size is now       Ÿ
                                    1512=            =    Ÿ  20K less the space needed for various PBUF control information  Ÿ
                                    1513=            =    Ÿ  (which is roughly 128 bytes).                                   Ÿ
